Saint-Etienne-du-Rouvray, slit his throat and took hostages before being shot dead by police. By: Express Web Desk | New Delhi | Updated: July 26, 2016 7:02 pm French soldiers and a police officer stand guard as they prevent the access to the scene of an attack in Saint Etienne du Rouvray, Normandy, France, Tuesday, July 26, 2016. Two attackers invaded a church Tuesday during morning Mass near the Normandy city of Rouen, killing an 84-year-old priest by slitting his throat and taking hostages before being shot and killed by police, French officials said. (AP Photo/Francois Mori) Top News Starry starry night: India gets its first astronomy resort Insulting question by TV anchor led to planning of PoK surgical strikes, says Manohar Parrikar Madras University to release UG, PG, professional degree results 2017 at unom.ac.in Archbishop Dominique Lebrun of Rouen has confirmed the identity of the priest who was slain by two attackers at a church in northwest France. He says 84-year-old Father Jacques Hamel was killed Tuesday. Police say two attackers entered his church in the small Normandy town of Saint-Etienne-du-Rouvray, slit his throat and took hostages before being shot dead by police. In a statement from Krakow, Poland, where Pope Francis was visiting, Lebrun says  I cry out to God, with all men of good will. And I invite all non-believers to unite with this cry & The Catholic Church has no other arms besides prayer and fraternity between men.  Two attackers seized hostages in a church near the Normandy city of Rouen on Tuesday, killing one hostage by slitting their throat before being killed by police, a security official said. The identities of the attackers and motive for the attack are unclear, according to the official, who was not authorized to be publicly named. French President Francois Hollande and Interior Minister Bernard Cazeneuve are en route to the town of Saint-Etienne-en-Rouvray where the hostage-taking took place, Interior Ministry spokesman Pierre-Henry Brandet said on France-Info radio. Anti-terrorism investigators have been summoned in the case, Brandet said. The incident comes as France is under high alert after an attack in Nice that killed 84 people and a string of deadly attacks last year claimed by the Islamic State group. France is also under a state of emergency and has extra police presence in the wake of the July 14 Nice attack. READ: Normandy after Nice: List of terrorist attacks across the globe in 2016 French Prime Minister Manuel Valls expressed his horror at what he called  a barbaric attack on a church .  The whole of France and all Catholics are wounded. We will stand together,  he wrote on Twitter. Mohammed Karabila, head of the Regional Council of the Muslim Faith for Haute-Normandie, said French security services knew the name of one of the attackers.  The person who committed this odious act is known and he has been followed by the police for at least 1 1/2 years. He went to Turkey and security services were alerted after this,  he told The Associated Press by phone. He refused to divulge man s name and had no information on the second attacker. Is the Deepest View Yet Into the Orion Nebula gizmodo Deadspin Fusion Gizmodo Jalopnik Jezebel Kotaku Lifehacker The Root Video Sploid Paleofuture io9 Science Reviews Field Guide This Is the Deepest View Yet Into the Orion Nebula George Dvorsky7/12/16 9:30am Filed to: Space porn orion nebula space nebulae science astronomy 9 4 Edit Promote Share to Kinja Toggle Conversation tools Go to permalink Image: ESO/H. Drass et al. Astronomers working with the Very Large Telescope in Chile have captured the deepest view yet of the heart of the Orion Nebula. Wow. Located 1,350 light-years from the sun, the Orion Nebula star-formation measures about 24 light-years across. Itï¿½\"s visible to the naked eye, appearing as a fuzzy patch in Orionï¿½\"s sword. Like other nebulae, Orion is illuminated by the many hot stars that are spawned within it, along with the glowing plasma clouds that have been stripped of their electrons from the ensuing ultraviolet radiation. Image: ESO/H. Drass et al. Scientists used the HAWK-I infrared instrument mounted to the VLT to capture this image, but it produced more than just a pretty picture. The new survey has revealed a treasure trove of low-mass objects, suggesting this stellar expanse is probably forming more low-mass objects than star formation regions. Close-ups of the Orion Nebula. Image: ESO/H. Drass et al. Observations show that there are more planet-sized objects within this region than previously thought. The researchers also found about ten times as many brown dwarfs (objects that blur the line between gas giants and stars) compared to previous surveys. Advertisement Advertisement Click here for a full resolution image. [Royal Astronomical Society] George Dvorsky @dvorsky George is a contributing editor at Gizmodo and io9. Share on Facebook(46k shares) Share on Twitter Share via email ijr 244k views Bernie Wants Heads to Roll After DNC Emails Show Election Rigged for Hillary--And He's Naming Names By Virginia Kruta a year ago Share on Facebook(46k shares) Share on Twitter Joe Raedle/Getty Images On Friday afternoon, Wikileaks dumped a number of emails from the Democratic National Committee (DNC). Some were emails sent by DNC employees to members of the media, and others were internal memos within the Democrat's party structure   but most of them raised a few questions. One of the recurring themes among many of those emails was Senator Bernie Sanders   specifically, how to undermine and discredit his presidential campaign in order to prevent him from winning the nomination. Senator Sanders appeared on CNN's  State of the Union  with Jake Tapper on Sunday morning to discuss the issue. The former presidential candidate had some harsh words for the DNC leadership: Bernie Sanders on DNC leak revelations: \"It's outrageous, but it is not a great shock\" #CNNSOTU https://t.co/dmk8qYpMqc  CNN (@CNN) July 24, 2016 He reminded viewers that he said Debbie Wasserman-Schultz should resign months ago, and he reiterated it Sunday morning. He also noted that the leaked emails were not the only reasons for his view:  I don't believe that she is qualified. We need to reach out to young people and the current leadership isn't doing that.  Sanders' campaign manager Jeff Weaver said on Saturday that someone within the DNC needed to be held responsible for the leaked emails. A number of Sanders' supporters have also called for Schultz's resignation. Saint-Etienne-du-Rouvray, slit his throat and took hostages before being shot dead by police. By: Express Web Desk | New Delhi | Updated: July 26, 2016 7:02 pm French soldiers and a police officer stand guard as they prevent the access to the scene of an attack in Saint Etienne du Rouvray, Normandy, France, Tuesday, July 26, 2016. Two attackers invaded a church Tuesday during morning Mass near the Normandy city of Rouen, killing an 84-year-old priest by slitting his throat and taking hostages before being shot and killed by police, French officials said. (AP Photo/Francois Mori) Top News Starry starry night: India gets its first astronomy resort Insulting question by TV anchor led to planning of PoK surgical strikes, says Manohar Parrikar Madras University to release UG, PG, professional degree results 2017 at unom.ac.in Archbishop Dominique Lebrun of Rouen has confirmed the identity of the priest who was slain by two attackers at a church in northwest France. He says 84-year-old Father Jacques Hamel was killed Tuesday. Police say two attackers entered his church in the small Normandy town of Saint-Etienne-du-Rouvray, slit his throat and took hostages before being shot dead by police. In a statement from Krakow, Poland, where Pope Francis was visiting, Lebrun says  I cry out to God, with all men of good will. And I invite all non-believers to unite with this cry & The Catholic Church has no other arms besides prayer and fraternity between men.  Two attackers seized hostages in a church near the Normandy city of Rouen on Tuesday, killing one hostage by slitting their throat before being killed by police, a security official said. The identities of the attackers and motive for the attack are unclear, according to the official, who was not authorized to be publicly named. French President Francois Hollande and Interior Minister Bernard Cazeneuve are en route to the town of Saint-Etienne-en-Rouvray where the hostage-taking took place, Interior Ministry spokesman Pierre-Henry Brandet said on France-Info radio. Anti-terrorism investigators have been summoned in the case, Brandet said. The incident comes as France is under high alert after an attack in Nice that killed 84 people and a string of deadly attacks last year claimed by the Islamic State group. France is also under a state of emergency and has extra police presence in the wake of the July 14 Nice attack. READ: Normandy after Nice: List of terrorist attacks across the globe in 2016 French Prime Minister Manuel Valls expressed his horror at what he called  a barbaric attack on a church .  The whole of France and all Catholics are wounded. We will stand together,  he wrote on Twitter. Mohammed Karabila, head of the Regional Council of the Muslim Faith for Haute-Normandie, said French security services knew the name of one of the attackers.  The person who committed this odious act is known and he has been followed by the police for at least 1 1/2 years. He went to Turkey and security services were alerted after this,  he told The Associated Press by phone. He refused to divulge man s name and had no information on the second attacker. Is the Deepest View Yet Into the Orion Nebula gizmodo Deadspin Fusion Gizmodo Jalopnik Jezebel Kotaku Lifehacker The Root Video Sploid Paleofuture io9 Science Reviews Field Guide This Is the Deepest View Yet Into the Orion Nebula George Dvorsky7/12/16 9:30am Filed to: Space porn orion nebula space nebulae science astronomy 9 4 Edit Promote Share to Kinja Toggle Conversation tools Go to permalink Image: ESO/H. Drass et al. Astronomers working with the Very Large Telescope in Chile have captured the deepest view yet of the heart of the Orion Nebula. Wow. Located 1,350 light-years from the sun, the Orion Nebula star-formation measures about 24 light-years across. Itï¿½\"s visible to the naked eye, appearing as a fuzzy patch in Orionï¿½\"s sword. Like other nebulae, Orion is illuminated by the many hot stars that are spawned within it, along with the glowing plasma clouds that have been stripped of their electrons from the ensuing ultraviolet radiation. Image: ESO/H. Drass et al. Scientists used the HAWK-I infrared instrument mounted to the VLT to capture this image, but it produced more than just a pretty picture. The new survey has revealed a treasure trove of low-mass objects, suggesting this stellar expanse is probably forming more low-mass objects than star formation regions. Close-ups of the Orion Nebula. Image: ESO/H. Drass et al. Observations show that there are more planet-sized objects within this region than previously thought. The researchers also found about ten times as many brown dwarfs (objects that blur the line between gas giants and stars) compared to previous surveys. Advertisement Advertisement Click here for a full resolution image. [Royal Astronomical Society] George Dvorsky @dvorsky George is a contributing editor at Gizmodo and io9.
